332026-03-08T20:04:00.611473agentmessage-
The answer file has been created at `/workspace/answer.json`. Here's a summary of my findings:

## Summary

I searched `github.com/scikit-learn/scikit-learn` for three structured logging/warning mechanisms:

### 1. `ConvergenceWarning`
- **Defined** in `sklearn/exceptions.py` as a `UserWarning` subclass
- **Raised** across 20+ source files whenever iterative algorithms hit `max_iter` without converging:
  - Linear models: `_cd_fast.pyx`, `_sag.py`, `_ridge.py`, `_ransac.py`, `_quantile.py`, `_theil_sen.py`, `_least_angle.py`, `_stochastic_gradient.py`, `_glm/_newton_solver.py`
  - SVM: `_base.py`; Clustering: `_affinity_propagation.py`, `_birch.py`, `_kmeans.py`
  - Mixture: `_base.py`; Decomposition: `_fastica.py`, `_factor_analysis.py`, `_nmf.py`
  - Neural networks: `_multilayer_perceptron.py`; Gaussian processes: `kernels.py`
  - Covariance: `_graph_lasso.py`; Cross decomposition: `_pls.py`
  - Shared optimizer utilities: `sklearn/utils/optimize.py`

### 2. `check_is_fitted` Warning
- **Defined** in `sklearn/utils/validation.py` — raises `NotFittedError` (from `sklearn/exceptions.py`) when inference methods are called before `fit()`

### 3. Verbose Parameter Logging
- **Core utility**: `sklearn/utils/_user_interface.py` — `_message_with_time()` and `_print_elapsed_time()` context manager
- **VerboseReporter class**: `sklearn/ensemble/_gb.py` — structured progress reporting for gradient boosting
- **Mixture model verbose methods**: `sklearn/mixture/_base.py` — `_print_verbose_msg_init_beg/iter_end/init_end`
- **Estimator-level `self.verbose`**: Used across `sklearn/pipeline.py`, `sklearn/model_selection/_search.py`, `sklearn/manifold/_t_sne.py`, `sklearn/impute/_iterative.py`, and many more

Verbose Parameter Logging\\n\\nThe verbose logging infrastructure is implemented at multiple levels:\\n\\n- **Core utility**: `sklearn/utils/_user_interface.py` provides `_message_with_time(source, message, time)` and the context manager `_print_elapsed_time(source, message)` for timing-based logging used in `sklearn/pipeline.py` and other meta-estimators.\\n- **VerboseReporter**: `sklearn/ensemble/_gb.py` defines the `VerboseReporter` class that reports training progress for gradient boosting estimators.\\n- **Mixture model verbose methods**: `sklearn/mixture/_base.py` implements `_print_verbose_msg_init_beg`, `_print_verbose_msg_iter_end`, and `_print_verbose_msg_init_end` for EM algorithm progress reporting.\\n- **Estimator-level verbose**: Many estimators store `self.verbose` and pass it to underlying solvers or use it to control `print()` calls: `sklearn/linear_model/_glm/_newton_solver.py`, `sklearn/linear_model/_theil_sen.py`, `sklearn/linear_model/_bayes.py`, `sklearn/cluster/_kmeans.py`, `sklearn/cluster/_affinity_propagation.py`, `sklearn/neighbors/_nca.py`, `sklearn/neural_network/_multilayer_perceptron.py`, `sklearn/neural_network/_rbm.py`, `sklearn/decomposition/_dict_learning.py`, `sklearn/covariance/_graph_lasso.py`, `sklearn/manifold/_t_sne.py`, `sklearn/impute/_iterative.py`, `sklearn/ensemble/_gb.py`, `sklearn/model_selection/_search.py`, `sklearn/pipeline.py`.\"\n}\nEOF\n\n\necho \"Done\"\nDone"
